## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="9f46a-1128">Atributos do Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9f46a-1128">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9f46a-1129">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9f46a-1129">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
